KG State Machine (TA State Values)\n\nThe `strState` array maps TA state integers to system property strings:\n\n| TA State | Int | `knox.kg.state` value | Meaning |\n|----------|-----|-----------------------|---------|\n| 0 | `KG_STATE_PRENORMAL` | `\"Prenormal\"` | Initial / not enrolled |\n| 1 | `KG_STATE_CHECKING` | `\"Checking\"` | Verification in progress |\n| 2 | `KG_STATE_ACTIVE` | `\"Active\"` | KG enrolled, not locked |\n| 3 | `KG_STATE_LOCKED` | `\"Locked\"` | KG locked (your device) |\n| 4 | `KG_STATE_COMPLETED` | `\"Completed\"` | KG process completed / unlocked |\n| 5 | `KG_STATE_ERROR` | `\"Error\"` | Error state |\n\nThe state is stored in **TrustZone RPMB** (Replay Protected Memory Block), read via `KnoxGuardNative.tz_getTAState(0)`, then written to system property `knox.kg.state` by `Utils.getStateAndSetToKGSystemProperty()`.\n\n### 2. Permission Check Architecture (`checkCallerAndKgPermission`)\n\nTwo checks are performed on every public method of `KnoxGuardSeService`:\n\n1. **`checkCaller()`** -- Verifies the calling UID's package name equals `\"com.samsung.android.kgclient\"`. Uses `context.getPackageManager().getNameForUid(Binder.getCallingUid())`.\n2. **`checkPermission()`** -- Calls `context.checkCallingPermission(\"com.samsung.android.knoxguard.STATUS\") == 0`. This uses `checkCallingPermission`, NOT `checkCallingOrSelfPermission`.\n\n**Critical distinction:** `checkCallingPermission()` checks the *remote caller's* UID. When called in-process (same process as system_server), `Binder.getCallingUid()` returns the caller's UID from the Binder transaction. But since the droppedapk runs IN system_server as UID 1000, and `checkCallingPermission` specifically checks the *calling* identity (not self), this matters for how you invoke it.\n\n### 3. IKnoxGuardManager Binder Interface (All 41 Transactions)\n\nKey transactions for KG removal:\n\n| TX | Method | Purpose |\n|----|--------|---------|\n| 13 | `getTAState()` | Read current TA state |\n| 22 | `unlockScreen()` | Calls `tz_unlockScreen` -- THE unlock method |\n| 28 | `resetRPMB()` | Reset RPMB storage |\n| 29 | `setCheckingState()` | Set state to Checking (calls `tz_userChecking`) |\n| 37 | `getKGServiceInfo()` | Returns Bundle with lock result + integrity |\n| 40 | `isKGAllowDO()` | Check if Device Owner allowed |\n| 41 | `isKGAllowADB()` | Check if ADB allowed |\n\n**Previous handoff notes had a critical error:** TX 36 is `isVpnExceptionRequired()` (returns boolean), NOT a disable command. TX 37 is `getKGServiceInfo()` (returns Bundle), NOT an enable command.\n\n### 4. KG Lock State Storage\n\nState is stored at **three levels**:\n\n1. **TrustZone TA (RPMB)** -- Primary authoritative state. Read via `tz_getTAState()`, written via `tz_lockScreen()` / `tz_unlockScreen()`. This survives factory resets. You cannot modify RPMB from userspace.\n\n2. **System property** `knox.kg.state` -- Transient, set by `Utils.getStateAndSetToKGSystemProperty()` on boot from TA state. Just a cache. Changing this alone does nothing because it gets re-read from TA on boot.\n\n3. **OTP fuse bit** `ro.boot.kg.bit` -- Hardware fuse read at boot. Values: `\"00\"` (first boot), `\"01\"` (KG enabled), `\"11\"` (KG completed), `\"FF\"` (unknown). This is a real OTP fuse -- it's permanent once burned.\n\nThere are **no files, databases, or SharedPreferences** in the service itself that store lock state. The `kgclient` app (`/data/data/com.samsung.android.kgclient/`) has its own data, but clearing it triggers error 3001 (data cleared detection) via `SystemIntentProcessor.handlePackageDataCleared()`.\n\n### 6. Error 8133 / Abnormal Detection\n\nError 8133 is not in the service-side code itself. It appears to be a **kgclient-side** error code that the KG client app reports when it detects tampering. The relevant service-side error codes are:\n\n- `3001` -- `ERROR_CLIENT_APP_DATA_CLEARED` (data cleared)\n- `3020` -- `ERROR_CLIENT_INTEGRITY` (integrity check failed)\n- `3040` -- `ERROR_CLIENT_INTEGRITY_FOR_CHINA`\n- `1001` -- `ERROR_KGTA_INIT_FAILED`\n- `1002` -- `ERROR_KGTA_APSERIAL_FAILED`\n- `1003` -- `ERROR_KGTA_RPMB_UNAVAILABLE`\n- `1004` -- `ERROR_KGTA_HMAC_MISMATCH`\n- `2002` -- `ERROR_RETRY_LOCK_DEFAULT`\n- `2003` -- `ERROR_LOCK_FROM_USER_PRESENT`\n\n`SystemIntentProcessor.handleBootCompleted()` checks TA integrity and AP serial on every boot, and calls `lockSeDevice()` if any check fails.
